{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define P\+S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+cfC(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{M,  }\item[{}]{I,  }\item[{}]{A,  }\item[{}]{B,  }\item[{}]{C }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

{\bfseries Value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}
(C==\textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)? B=strlen(A):                \(\backslash\)
                    (A[C-1]=\textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'},B=strlen(A),memset((A)+B,\textcolor{charliteral}{' '},C-B-1),B=C-1));
\end{DoxyCode}
